SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."AppraiserId", t."CreatedAt", t."CycleId", t."EmployeeId", t."Status", t."SummaryId", t."Id0", t."AppraiseeScore", t."AppraiserScore", t."CycleId0", t."EmployeeId0", t."PerformanceBucket", t."Id1", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t."Id2", t."departmentId", t."EmployeeRoleCode", t."HierarchyLevel", t."RoleName", t."Id3", t."DepartmentName", t0."Id", t0."AppraiseeComment", t0."AppraiseeRating", t0."AppraiserComment", t0."AppraiserRating", t0."FeedbackId", t0."QuestionId", t0."Status", t0."Artifact_FilePath", t0."Artifact_FileType", t0."Id0", t0."PerformanceIndicatorId", t0."QuestionText", t0."Status0", t0."Id1", t0."FactorId", t0."IndicatorName", t0."Weightage", t0."Id2", t0."FactorName"
FROM (
    SELECT a."Id", a."AppraiserId", a."CreatedAt", a."CycleId", a."EmployeeId", a."Status", a."SummaryId", a0."Id" AS "Id0", a0."AppraiseeScore", a0."AppraiserScore", a0."CycleId" AS "CycleId0", a0."EmployeeId" AS "EmployeeId0", a0."PerformanceBucket", e."Id" AS "Id1", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber", e0."Id" AS "Id2", e0."departmentId", e0."EmployeeRoleCode", e0."HierarchyLevel", e0."RoleName", d."Id" AS "Id3", d."DepartmentName"
    FROM appraisal_feedbacks AS a
    LEFT JOIN appraisal_summaries AS a0 ON a."SummaryId" = a0."Id"
    INNER JOIN employees AS e ON a."EmployeeId" = e."Id"
    INNER JOIN employee_roles AS e0 ON e."EmployeeRoleId" = e0."Id"
    INNER JOIN department AS d ON e0."departmentId" = d."Id"
    WHERE a."EmployeeId" = @__employeeId_0 AND a."CycleId" = @__cycleId_1
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a1."Id", a1."AppraiseeComment", a1."AppraiseeRating", a1."AppraiserComment", a1."AppraiserRating", a1."FeedbackId", a1."QuestionId", a1."Status", a1."Artifact_FilePath", a1."Artifact_FileType", q."Id" AS "Id0", q."PerformanceIndicatorId", q."QuestionText", q."Status" AS "Status0", p."Id" AS "Id1", p."FactorId", p."IndicatorName", p."Weightage", p0."Id" AS "Id2", p0."FactorName"
    FROM appraisal_feedback_details AS a1
    INNER JOIN question AS q ON a1."QuestionId" = q."Id"
    INNER JOIN performance_indicator AS p ON q."PerformanceIndicatorId" = p."Id"
    INNER JOIN performance_factor AS p0 ON p."FactorId" = p0."Id"
    WHERE a1."Status" = 'Pending' OR a1."Status" = 'UnderReview'
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."FeedbackId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t."Id0", t."Id1", t."Id2", t."Id3", t0."Id", t0."Id0", t0."Id1"

    LEFT JOIN appraisal_summaries AS a0 ON a."SummaryId" = a0."Id"
    INNER JOIN employees AS e ON a."EmployeeId" = e."Id"
    INNER JOIN employee_roles AS e0 ON e."EmployeeRoleId" = e0."Id"
    INNER JOIN department AS d ON e0."departmentId" = d."Id"
    WHERE a."EmployeeId" = @__employeeId_0 AND a."CycleId" = @__cycleId_1
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a1."Id", a1."AppraiseeComment", a1."AppraiseeRating", a1."AppraiserComment", a1."AppraiserRating", a1."FeedbackId", a1."QuestionId", a1."Status", a1."Artifact_FilePath", a1."Artifact_FileType", q."Id" AS "Id0", q."PerformanceIndicatorId", q."QuestionText", q."Status" AS "Status0", p."Id" AS "Id1", p."FactorId", p."IndicatorName", p."Weightage", p0."Id" AS "Id2", p0."FactorName"
    FROM appraisal_feedback_details AS a1

    WHERE a1."Status" = 'Pending' OR a1."Status" = 'UnderReview'
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."FeedbackId"

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace

                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s0."SystemRoleId", s0."PermissionId", p."Id", p."PermissionCode", p."PermissionName"
        FROM systemrole_permissions AS s0
        INNER JOIN permissions AS p ON s0."PermissionId" = p."Id"
    ) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SystemRoleId"
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."EmployeeId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedOn", t."Email", t."EmployeeRoleId", t."FirstName", t."IsActive", t."LastName", t."ModifiedOn", t."PasswordHash", t."PhoneNumber", t0."EmployeeId", t0."SystemRoleId", t0."Id", t0.description, t0.role_name, t0."SystemRoleId0", t0."PermissionId", t0."Id0", t0."PermissionCode", t0."PermissionName"
FROM (
    SELECT e."Id", e."CreatedOn", e."Email", e."EmployeeRoleId", e."FirstName", e."IsActive", e."LastName", e."ModifiedOn", e."PasswordHash", e."PhoneNumber"
    FROM employees AS e
    WHERE e."Email" = @__email_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT e0."EmployeeId", e0."SystemRoleId", s."Id", s.description, s.role_name, t1."SystemRoleId" AS "SystemRoleId0", t1."PermissionId", t1."Id" AS "Id0", t1."PermissionCode", t1."PermissionName"
    FROM employees_systemroles_mapping AS e0
    INNER JOIN system_roles AS s ON e0."SystemRoleId" = s."Id"
    LEFT JOIN (

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

) AS t
